    SELECT [e7].[Id], [e7].[PLU], [e7].[Name], [e7].[CategoryId], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [e5].[Symbol]
        FROM [Emenu_Currency] AS [e5]
        WHERE ([e5].[Currency] = [e7].[Currency]) OR ([e5].[Currency] IS NULL AND [e7].[Currency] IS NULL)) AS [c], [e7].[Price], CONVERT(VARCHAR(100), [e7].[Price]) AS [c0], [e7].[DetailsEN], CASE
        WHEN [e7].[ThumbnailImageName] IS NOT NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
        ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
    END AS [c1], [e7].[ThumbnailImageName], CASE
        WHEN [e7].[LargeImageName] IS NOT NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
        ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
    END AS [c2], [e7].[LargeImageName], [e7].[LargeDetailsEN], CASE
        WHEN [e7].[OverLayImageName] IS NOT NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
        ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
    END AS [c3], [e7].[OverLayImageName], [e7].[OverlayDetailsEN], [e7].[CommentsEN], [e7].[LabelEN], [e6].[Id] AS [Id0], [t1].[Id] AS [Id1], [t1].[Name] AS [Name0], [t1].[Status], [t1].[c] AS [c4], [t1].[IconTagName], [t1].[LabelEN] AS [LabelEN0], [t1].[Id0] AS [Id00], [e6].[EMenusId]

        SELECT [e9].[Id], [e9].[Name], [e9].[Status], CASE
            WHEN [e9].[IconTagName] IS NOT NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)

        END AS [c], [e9].[IconTagName], [e9].[LabelEN], [e8].[Id] AS [Id0], [e8].[EMenuItemId]

        INNER JOIN [Emenu_ItemTags] AS [e9] ON [e8].[ItemTagId] = [e9].[Id]
        WHERE ([e9].[IsDeleted] <> CAST(1 AS bit)) AND ([e9].[Status] = CAST(1 AS bit))
    ) AS [t1] ON [e7].[Id] = [t1].[EMenuItemId]
    WHERE ([e7].[IsDeleted] <> CAST(1 AS bit)) AND ([e7].[Status] = CAST(1 AS bit))
) AS [t2] ON [t].[Id0] = [t2].[EMenusId]
